   984:   function aicmOrgUpdateBodyRows(body) {
   985:     var keys = Object.keys(body || {}).filter(function (key) {
   986:       return key !== "owner_civilization_id" &&
   987:         key.indexOf("_id") === -1 &&
   988:         key !== "aicm_user_company_id" &&
   989:         key !== "aicm_user_company_department_id" &&

  1038:   async function executeAicmOrgUpdateConfirm() {
  1039:     var payload = state.pendingOrgUpdate || null;
  1040: 
  1041:     if (!payload || !payload.endpoint || !payload.body) {
  1042:       setMessage("error", "確認対象がありません。");
  1043:       return;
  1044:     }
  1045: 
  1046:     try {
  1047:       await aicmOrgPostJson(payload.endpoint, payload.body);
  1048:             // AICM_AXC_EXECUTE_ROLE_PLACEMENT_SYNC_AFTER_MAIN_UPDATE
  1049:       await aicmAxcSyncRolePlacementsForPayload(payload);
  1050: state.pendingOrgUpdate = null;
  1051:       // AICM_PRESERVE_UNSAVED_WORKER_ADD_AXO_V1
  1052:       if (typeof aicmAxoClearDraftAfterSuccessfulSave === "function") aicmAxoClearDraftAfterSuccessfulSave();

  1620: function aicmPlacementMatchesRole(row, roleCode) {

  1629:     }
  1630: 
  1631:     if (roleCode === "leader") {

  1633:     }
  1634: 
  1635:     if (roleCode === "worker") {
  1636:       return text.indexOf("worker") >= 0 || text.indexOf("従業員") >= 0 || text.indexOf("ワーカー") >= 0;
  1637:     }
  1638: 
  1639:     return false;
  1640:   }

  1658: function aicmRoleScopeMatches(row, scope) {

  1660: 
  1661:     if (scope.companyId && row.aicm_user_company_id && row.aicm_user_company_id !== scope.companyId) return false;
  1662: 
  1663:     if (scope.departmentId) {
  1664:       var rowDepartmentId = row.aicm_user_company_department_id || row.department_id || "";
  1665:       if (rowDepartmentId && rowDepartmentId !== scope.departmentId) return false;
  1666:     }
  1667:

  1669:       var rowSectionId = row.aicm_user_company_section_id || row.section_id || "";
  1670:       if (rowSectionId && rowSectionId !== scope.sectionId) return false;
  1671:     }
  1672: 
  1673:     return true;
  1674:   }

  3697: function downloadTextFile(filename, text, mimeType) {
  3698:     var blob = new Blob([String(text || "")], { type: mimeType || "text/plain;charset=utf-8" });
  3699:     var url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
  3700:     var a = document.createElement("a");
  3701:     a.href = url;
  3702:     a.download = filename;
  3703:     document.body.appendChild(a);
  3704:     a.click();
  3705:     a.remove();
  3706:     setTimeout(function () {
  3707:       URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
  3708:     }, 1000);
  3709:   }

  4216: 
  4217: function renderPmlwMajorRows(rows) {
  4218:     // AICM_AXU_CSV_R8_RENDER_PMLW_MAJOR_ROWS_REPAIR_V1
  4219:     function h(value) {
  4220:       if (typeof escapeHtml === "function") return escapeHtml(value);
  4221:       return String(value == null ? "" : value)
  4222:         .replace(/&/g, "&amp;")
  4223:         .replace(/</g, "&lt;")
  4224:         .replace(/>/g, "&gt;")
  4225:         .replace(/"/g, "&quot;")
  4226:         .replace(/'/g, "&#39;");
  4227:     }
  4228: 
  4229:     function value(row, keys, fallback) {
  4230:       for (var i = 0; i < keys.length; i += 1) {
  4231:         var key = keys[i];
  4232:         if (row && row[key] != null && String(row[key]) !== "") return row[key];
  4233:       }
  4234:       return fallback == null ? "" : fallback;
  4235:     }
  4236: 
  4237:     function rowId(row, index) {
  4238:       if (typeof aicmAxuR1MajorId === "function") {
  4239:         var id = aicmAxuR1MajorId(row);
  4240:         if (id) return id;
  4241:       }
  4242: 
  4243:       return String(
  4244:         value(row, [
  4245:           "aicm_manager_major_work_item_id",
  4246:           "manager_major_work_item_id",
  4247:           "pmlw_major_item_id",
  4248:           "major_item_id",
  4249:           "id"
  4250:         ], "row-" + String(index))
  4251:       );
  4252:     }
  4253: 
  4254:     var list = Array.isArray(rows) ? rows : [];
  4255: 
  4256:     if (!list.length && typeof selectedCompany === "function" && typeof pmlwMajorRowsForCompany === "function") {
  4257:       var company = selectedCompany();
  4258:       list = company ? pmlwMajorRowsForCompany(company.aicm_user_company_id) : [];
  4259:     }
  4260: 
  4261:     if (!Array.isArray(list) || list.length === 0) {
  4262:       return [
  4263:         '<div class="aicm-empty-state">',
  4264:         '  <strong>登録済み大項目はまだありません</strong>',
  4265:         '  <p>President起点でAI企業業務を開始するか、CSVで部長/Manager分解済みの大項目を取り込むと、ここに表示されます。</p>',
  4266:         '</div>'
  4267:       ].join("");
  4268:     }
  4269:

  4318: function aicmGetManagerMajorRowsForSelectedCompany(companyId) {
  4319:     // AICM_MANAGER_MAJOR_PENDING_DISPLAY_CANONICAL_V1: rows
  4320:     var ctx = state && state.context ? state.context : {};
  4321:     var selectedId = String(companyId || "");
  4322: 
  4323:     if (!selectedId && state && state.selectedCompanyId) {
  4324:       selectedId = String(state.selectedCompanyId || "");
  4325:     }
  4326: 
  4327:     if (!selectedId && typeof selectedCompany === "function") {
  4328:       var company = selectedCompany();
  4329:       if (company && company.aicm_user_company_id) {
  4330:         selectedId = String(company.aicm_user_company_id || "");
  4331:       }
  4332:     }
  4333: 
  4334:     function asArray(value) {
  4335:       return Array.isArray(value) ? value : [];
  4336:     }
  4337: 
  4338:     function rowCompanyId(row) {
  4339:       return String(
  4340:         row && (
  4341:           row.aicm_user_company_id ||
  4342:           row.company_id ||
  4343:           row.user_company_id ||
  4344:           row.companyId ||
  4345:           ""
  4346:         ) || ""
  4347:       );
  4348:     }
  4349: 
  4350:     function statusText(row, keys) {
  4351:       for (var i = 0; i < keys.length; i += 1) {
  4352:         var key = keys[i];
  4353:         if (row && row[key] != null && String(row[key]) !== "") {
  4354:           return String(row[key]).toLowerCase();
  4355:         }
  4356:       }
  4357: 
  4358:       return "";
  4359:     }
  4360: 
  4361:     function isPendingMajor(row) {
  4362:       var handoff = statusText(row, ["handoff_status_code", "handoff_status", "leader_handoff_status_code"]);
  4363:       var decomposition = statusText(row, ["decomposition_status_code", "work_status_code", "status_code"]);
  4364: 
  4365:       var closed = {
  4366:         sent: true,
  4367:         handed_off: true,
  4368:         leader_handoff_done: true,
  4369:         submitted: true,
  4370:         delivered: true,
  4371:         done: true,
  4372:         completed: true,
  4373:         complete: true,
  4374:         cancelled: true,
  4375:         canceled: true,
  4376:         archived: true
  4377:       };
  4378: 
  4379:       if (closed[handoff]) return false;
  4380:       if (closed[decomposition]) return false;
  4381: 
  4382:       return true;
  4383:     }
  4384: 
  4385:     function rowOrder(row) {
  4386:       var n = Number(row && (row.display_order || row.sort_order || row.row_order || 0));
  4387:       return Number.isFinite(n) ? n : 0;
  4388:     }
  4389: 
  4390:     var rows = []
  4391:       .concat(asArray(ctx.pmlw_major_items))
  4392:       .concat(asArray(ctx.manager_major_items))
  4393:       .concat(asArray(ctx.major_items));
  4394: 
  4395:     rows = rows.filter(function (row) {
  4396:       if (!row) return false;
  4397: 
  4398:       var cid = rowCompanyId(row);
  4399: 
  4400:       if (selectedId && cid && cid !== selectedId) return false;
  4401: 
  4402:       return isPendingMajor(row);
  4403:     });
  4404: 
  4405:     rows.sort(function (a, b) {
  4406:       var ao = rowOrder(a);
  4407:       var bo = rowOrder(b);
  4408: 
  4409:       if (ao !== bo) return ao - bo;
  4410: 
  4411:       var an = String((a && (a.major_item_name || a.title || a.task_name || a.deliverable_name)) || "");
  4412:       var bn = String((b && (b.major_item_name || b.title || b.task_name || b.deliverable_name)) || "");
  4413: 
  4414:       return an.localeCompare(bn, "ja");
  4415:     });
  4416: 
  4417:     return rows;
  4418:   }

  7464:   function aicmManagerMajorSummaryRowsR8U() {

  7470:     function add(list) {
  7471:       if (!Array.isArray(list)) return;
  7472:       for (var i = 0; i < list.length; i += 1) {
  7473:         var row = list[i];
  7474:         if (!row || typeof row !== "object") continue;

  7484:       }

  7487:     add(ctx.pmlw_major_items);
  7488:     add(ctx.pmlwMajorItems);

 10358: async function aicmRuntimeStatusRefresh() {
 10359:     state.runtimeStatusLoading = true;
 10360:     state.runtimeStatusError = "";
 10361: 
 10362:     if (typeof render === "function") render();
 10363: 
 10364:     try {
 10365:       var response = await fetch("/api/aicm/v2/worker-runtime/pipeline-board?app_surface_code=ai_company_manager&source_app_ref=AICompanyManager", { method: "GET" });
 10366:       var json = await response.json();
 10367: 
 10368:       if (!response.ok || (json && json.result === "error")) {
 10369:         var message = (json && json.error_message) || "実行状況の取得に失敗しました。";
 10370:         throw new Error(message);
 10371:       }
 10372: 
 10373:       var runtimeRows = aicmRuntimeStatusRowsFromPayload(json);
 10374:       state.runtimeStatusRawRows = runtimeRows;
 10375:       state.runtimeStatusRows = aicmRuntimeStatusFilterRowsForCurrentApp(runtimeRows);
 10376:       state.runtimeStatusRaw = json;
 10377:       state.runtimeStatusUpdatedAt = new Date().toLocaleString();
 10378:       state.runtimeStatusLoading = false;
 10379:       state.runtimeStatusError = "";
 10380: 
 10381:       if (typeof render === "function") render();
 10382:     } catch (error) {
 10383:       state.runtimeStatusLoading = false;
 10384:       state.runtimeStatusError = error && error.message ? error.message : "実行状況の取得に失敗しました。";
 10385: 
 10386:       if (typeof render === "function") render();
 10387:     }
 10388:   }

 10448: function buildWorkerRuntimePendingPayload() {
 10449:     var company = aicmWrtCurrentCompany();
 10450:     if (!company) throw new Error("AI企業を選択してください。");
 10451: 
 10452:     var placementId = aicmWrtValue("aicm-worker-runtime-placement-id");
 10453:     if (!placementId) throw new Error("実行AI/AI/Workerを選択してください。");
 10454: 
 10455:     var worker = aicmWrtPlacementById(placementId);
 10456:     if (!worker) throw new Error("選択したWorker配置が見つかりません。");
 10457: 
 10458:     var title = aicmWrtValue("aicm-worker-runtime-title");
 10459:     if (!title) throw new Error("作業タイトルを入力してください。");
 10460: 
 10461:     var instruction = aicmWrtValue("aicm-worker-runtime-instruction");
 10462:     if (!instruction) throw new Error("作業指示を入力してください。");
 10463: 
 10464:     var sourceRef = aicmWrtValue("aicm-worker-runtime-source-ref") || aicmWrtDefaultSourceRequestRef();
 10465:     var idempotencyKey = aicmWrtBuildIdempotencyKey(sourceRef, placementId);
 10466: 
 10467:     return {
 10468:       endpoint: "/api/aicm/v2/worker-runtime/request",
 10469:       worker_label: aicmWrtWorkerLabel(worker),
 10470:       body: {
 10471:         owner_civilization_id: aicmWrtOwnerId(),
 10472:         aicm_user_company_id: aicmWrtText(company.aicm_user_company_id),
 10473:         aicm_user_company_department_id: aicmWrtText(worker.aicm_user_company_department_id),
 10474:         aicm_user_company_section_id: aicmWrtText(worker.aicm_user_company_section_id),
 10475:         aicm_user_company_worker_placement_id: placementId,
 10476:         model_code: aicmWrtText(worker.aiworker_model_code),
 10477:         robot_pool_id: aicmWrtText(worker.robot_pool_id),
 10478:         app_surface_code: "ai_company_manager",
 10479:         task_domain_code: aicmWrtValue("aicm-worker-runtime-task-domain") || "business_operation",
 10480:         task_title: title,
 10481:         task_instruction_ja: instruction,
 10482:         source_app_ref: "AICompanyManager",
 10483:         source_request_ref: sourceRef,
 10484:         requested_by_ref: "human",
 10485:         idempotency_key: idempotencyKey
 10486:       }
 10487:     };
 10488:   }

 10535: async function aicmWrtPostJson(path, body) {
 10536:     var response = await fetch(path, {
 10537:       method: "POST",
 10538:       headers: {
 10539:         "Content-Type": "application/json"
 10540:       },
 10541:       body: JSON.stringify(body || {})
 10542:     });
 10543: 
 10544:     var json = await response.json().catch(function () {
 10545:       return {};
 10546:     });
 10547: 
 10548:     if (!response.ok || !json || json.result !== "ok") {
 10549:       throw new Error((json && (json.error_message || json.message || json.error)) || "AI実行Workbenchに失敗しました。");
 10550:     }
 10551: 
 10552:     return json;
 10553:   }
 10554: 
 10555: async function executeWorkerRuntimeConfirmBaseAxtR9R1() {
 10556:     var payload = state.pendingWorkerRuntimeRequest || null;
 10557:     if (!payload || !payload.endpoint || !payload.body) {
 10558:       setMessage("error", "確認対象がありません。");
 10559:       return;
 10560:     }
 10561: 
 10562:     try {
 10563:       var result = await aicmWrtPostJson(payload.endpoint, payload.body);
 10564:       state.pendingWorkerRuntimeRequest = null;
 10565:       state.workerRuntimeLastResult = result;
 10566:       state.screen = "worker-runtime-request";
 10567:       setMessage("ok", "AI実行Workbenchを作成しました。");
 10568:       if (typeof render === "function") render();
 10569:     } catch (error) {
 10570:       setMessage("error", error && error.message ? error.message : "AI実行Workbenchに失敗しました。");
 10571:       if (typeof render === "function") render();
 10572:     }
 10573:   }
 10574: 
 10575: async function executeWorkerRuntimeConfirm() {
 10576:     // AICM_RUNTIME_STATUS_PANEL_AXT_R9_R1_V1

 10578: 
 10579:     setTimeout(function () {
 10580:       if (typeof aicmRuntimeStatusRefresh === "function") {
 10581:         aicmRuntimeStatusRefresh();
 10582:       }
 10583:     }, 250);
 10584: 
 10585:     return result;
 10586:   }

 10595:     } catch (error) {
 10596:       setMessage("error", error && error.message ? error.message : "確認画面を表示できません。");
 10597:       if (typeof render === "function") render();
 10598:     }
 10599:   }

 12592:     return String(value).trim();

 12595:   function esc(value) {
 12596:     var s = t(value);
 12597:     if (typeof escapeHtml === "function") return escapeHtml(s);
 12598:     return s
 12599:       .replace(/&/g, "&amp;")
 12600:       .replace(/</g, "&lt;")

 12606:   function first(row, keys, fallback) {
 12607:     row = row || {};
 12608:     for (var i = 0; i < keys.length; i += 1) {
 12609:       var key = keys[i];
 12610:       if (Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(row, key)) {
 12611:         var value = t(row[key]);
 12612:         if (value) return value;
 12613:       }
 12614:     }
 12615:     return fallback || "";
 12616:   }

 12618:   function normalize(appState, ctx) {
 12619:     appState = appState || {};
 12620:     if (!ctx || typeof ctx !== "object") ctx = {};
 12621: 
 12622:     var rows = [];
 12623:     if (Array.isArray(ctx.review_wait_items)) rows = ctx.review_wait_items;
 12624:     else if (Array.isArray(ctx.reviewWaitItems)) rows = ctx.reviewWaitItems;
 12625:     else if (Array.isArray(ctx.human_review_wait_items)) rows = ctx.human_review_wait_items;
 12626:     else if (Array.isArray(ctx.humanReviewWaitItems)) rows = ctx.humanReviewWaitItems;
 12627:     else if (Array.isArray(appState.review_wait_items)) rows = appState.review_wait_items;
 12628: 
 12629:     ctx.review_wait_items = rows;
 12630:     appState.context = ctx;
 12631:     appState.review_wait_items = rows;
 12632: 
 12633:     if (ctx.owner_civilization_id) appState.owner_civilization_id = ctx.owner_civilization_id;
 12634:     if (ctx.aicm_user_company_id) appState.selectedCompanyId = ctx.aicm_user_company_id;
 12635: 
 12636:     return ctx;
 12637:   }

 14186:     function installClickBridge() {

 14192:         while (target && target !== document && !target.getAttribute("data-core-action")) {
 14193:           target = target.parentNode;
 14194:         }

 14197: 
 14198:         var action = target.getAttribute("data-core-action");

 14200:

 14203:

 14205:

 14207:         if (action === "review-v10d-close-detail") return closeDetail();

 14234:       return text
 14235:         .replace(/&/g, "&amp;")

 14239:         .replace(/'/g, "&#039;");
 14240:     }

 14266:     function rowsFromPayload(payload) {
 14267:       payload = payload && typeof payload === "object" ? payload : {};
 14268:       var candidates = [
 14269:         payload.review_wait_items,
 14270:         payload.human_review_wait_items,
 14271:         payload.humanReviewWaitItems,
 14272:         payload.context && payload.context.review_wait_items,
 14273:         payload.data && payload.data.review_wait_items
 14274:       ];
 14275: 
 14276:       for (var i = 0; i < candidates.length; i += 1) {
 14277:         if (Array.isArray(candidates[i])) {
 14278:           return candidates[i].filter(function(row) {
 14279:             return row && typeof row === "object";
 14280:           });
 14281:         }
 14282:       }
 14283: 
 14284:       return [];
 14285:     }
 14286: 
 14287:     function rows(appState) {
 14288:       appState = app(appState);
 14289:       var c = ctx(appState);
 14290:       var r = rowsFromPayload(c);
 14291: 
 14292:       if (!r.length && Array.isArray(appState.review_wait_items)) r = appState.review_wait_items;
 14293: 
 14294:       var cid = companyId(appState);
 14295:       if (cid) {
 14296:         r = r.filter(function(row) {
 14297:           var rowCompany = t(row.aicm_user_company_id || row.company_id || row.companyId);
 14298:           return !rowCompany || rowCompany === cid;
 14299:         });
 14300:       }
 14301: 
 14302:       return r;
 14303:     }

 14306:       appState = app(appState);

 14310:

 14313:           c[key] = payload[key];
 14314:         });
 14315:       }
 14316: 
 14317:       if (r.length) {
 14318:         c.review_wait_items = r;
 14319:         appState.review_wait_items = r;
 14320:       }
 14321: 
 14322:       appState.aicmR8zV10d2PayloadRows = r.length;
 14323:       appState.aicmR8zV10d2MergedAt = new Date().toISOString();
 14324:       return r;
 14325:     }
